The wife and I own this cozy little house in a clean, quiet, middle-class neighborhood. Our house has been owned by our family since it was purchased new, in 1946. The wife and I have lived in it, ourselves, since 2003. We are fortunate in many respects. First of all, we have the best neighborhood you could imagine. We love our neighbors. They're the the best in the West. We exchange Christmas and birthday gifts with them. Our neighbors are all super friendly to our AIRbnb guests. Give ‘em a friendly smile and a wave. Let them know you are friendly, as well. If you are driving, please try to park directly in front of our house. Out of respect, our neighbors usually try to leave a space open for our guests - if at all possible. If you cannot find a space directly in front of our house, just give me a call and I will move my car around back and you can have my space. You should not have to rent a car but if you are bringing a car to park at our house please note the following weekly street-sweeping parking restriction: Do not park across our street (on the opposite side) on Mondays between the hours of 10 AM and 1 PM as posted on the warning signs on the street. Do not park on our side of the street between the hours of 10 AM and 1 PM Tuesdays as posted on the warning signs. Sometimes the warning signs are not nearby. The citation is just shy of $50. One more parking concern, if you're on our house side of the street your car must not face against the other cars but must park heading in the same, in other words just notice the Direction that the other cars are facing and do not park the opposite direction of the other cars on the same side of the street.
